              <script>
               jQuery(document).ready(function() {
	jQuery("#globalHeaderIncludeSm #promoslot-gps").slick({
		"lazyLoad": "progressive",
		"dots": false,
		"arrows": true,
		"infinite": true,
		"autoplay": true,
		"autoplaySpeed": 6000,
		"speed": 1500,
		"fade": true,
		"slidesToShow": 1,
		"slidesToScroll": 1
	});
	var cpwmCarouselContainerW = 0;
	var cpwmCarouselW = 0;
	var cpwmCarouselLmarg = 0;
	function cpwmSetMargin () {
		var cpwmCarouselContainerW = jQuery("#cpwm-carousel-p").width();
		var cpwmCarouselW = jQuery("#promoslot-gps").width();
		var cpwmCarouselLmarg = (cpwmCarouselContainerW - cpwmCarouselW) / 2;
//		console.log("Calculate: container- "+cpwmCarouselContainerW+"; carousel- "+cpwmCarouselW+", left margin- "+cpwmCarouselLmarg);
		jQuery("#promoslot-gps").css("margin-left",cpwmCarouselLmarg+"px");
	}
	cpwmSetMargin ();
	jQuery(window).resize(function() {
			cpwmSetMargin ();
	});
});
	jQuery(window).on("resize scroll",function(){
		var cpwmCarPosChk = jQuery(".ml-header-wrapper").css("position");
//		console.log("visible/invisible: " + cpwmCarPosChk);
		if(cpwmCarPosChk == "fixed") {
			jQuery("#globalHeaderIncludeSm").addClass("cpwmCarouselVisiblityNone");
		} else {
			jQuery("#globalHeaderIncludeSm").removeClass("cpwmCarouselVisiblityNone");
		}
	})
              </script>

function bannerdetails(){
	var bannerCTA = jQuery(".showbannerdisclaimer");
	var bannermodalDisclaimer = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.bannerdisclaimer");
	var bannercloseBtn = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.bannerdisclaimer");
	bannerCTA.click(function(){
//		console.log("BANNER CLICK");
		bannermodalDisclaimer.show();
	});
	bannercloseBtn.click(function(){
		bannermodalDisclaimer.hide();
	});
}

jQuery(document).ready(function(){
	bannerdetails();

		jQuery("#promoslot-gps a").attr("href", wishListApplyCode);

disclaimer selectors: 
promo-header: .promo-header .promoslot .promodetails
promo-directory: .directorydisclaimer
FOOTER_KICKER (promo bar): .shareddisclaimer
Home page: .discountdetails
Currently not used: .promo-directory .promoslot .promodetails
*/
    var isOrderLookup =  window.location.href.indexOf("wmorderlookup.do");
    if(isOrderLookup != -1) {
        jQuery(".cpwm-evergreen").hide();
        jQuery(".cpwm-orderlookup").show();
    }

	var cpwmTemplate = getUrlParameter("template");
	var cpwmSku = getUrlParameter("plfsku");
	var cpwmPromo = "";

    var cpwmLoc = window.location.href;
    if ((cpwmLoc.indexOf("/account/") != -1) && cpwmLoc.includes("?")) {
/*OUT4NOW        var cpwmCode = $("#promoslot-gps a").attr("href");
        cpwmLoc = cpwmLoc + "&" + cpwmCode.substring(1,cpwmCode.length);
        jQuery("#promoslot-gps a").attr("href", cpwmLoc);*/
    } else if (cpwmTemplate == "PLA") {
		var cpwmCode = $("#promoslot-gps a").attr("href");
		var cpwmBannerCode = "";
		if($("#pdpBanner a").attr("href")){
			cpwmBannerCode = $("#pdpBanner a").attr("href");
		}
		cpwmLoc = cpwmLoc.split("?");
		cpwmBaseLoc = cpwmLoc[0];
		cpwmLoc = cpwmBaseLoc + "?template=PLA&plfsku=" + cpwmSku + "&" + cpwmCode.substring(1,cpwmCode.length);
		var cpwmLocBanner = "";
		if(cpwmBannerCode && cpwmBannerCode.indexOf("template=PLA") == -1){
			cpwmLocBanner = cpwmBaseLoc + "?template=PLA&plfsku=" + cpwmSku + "&" + cpwmBannerCode.substring(1,cpwmBannerCode.length);
			jQuery("#pdpBanner a").attr("href", cpwmLocBanner);
		}
/*OUT4NOW		jQuery("#promoslot-gps a").attr("href", cpwmLoc);*/
		
    }

    var detailsCTA = jQuery(".promo-directory .promoslot .promodetails, .promo-header .promoslot .promodetails, .directorydisclaimer, .shareddisclaimer, .discountdetails, #see-details, #globalHeaderIncludeSm .shareddisclaimer");
	var modalDisclaimer = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.disclaimer")
    var alternatedetailsCTA = jQuery(".directoryalternatedisclaimer, .banneralternatedisclaimer, #globalHeaderIncludeSm .directoryalternatedisclaimer");
	var alternatemodalDisclaimer = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.alternatedisclaimer");
	var closeBtn = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.disclaimer, .cpwm-promo-modal.alternatedisclaimer");
    detailsCTA.click(function(){
//		console.log("Disclaimer click");
        modalDisclaimer.show();
    });
    alternatedetailsCTA.click(function(){
//		console.log("Alternate Disclaimer Click");
        alternatemodalDisclaimer.show();
    });
    closeBtn.click(function(){
        modalDisclaimer.hide();
		alternatemodalDisclaimer.hide();
    });
    var stateForWine = getStateFromDomHeader();
    if(document.getElementById("cpwm-bwol-puis")) {
        if(stateForWine == "CA") {
            jQuery("#cpwm-bwol-puis").show();
        }
    }
    if(document.getElementById("winesale")) {
        if(stateForWine != "CA") {
            jQuery(".ml-wm-freeshipping").hide();
        }
    }
});
function getStateFromDomHeader() {
    var state = '';
    var address2 = jQuery(".eslAddress2").html();
    if(address2 != undefined && address2 != "undefined" && address2 != '') {
        var addressToken = address2.split(" ");
        if(addressToken != null && (addressToken.length > 2)) {
            state = addressToken[addressToken.length - 2]
        }
    }
    return state;
}

              // Function Include - General Utility to include a javascript file
// should be integrated with global.js when ready
function include(file) {
    var script  = document.createElement('script');
    script.src  = file;
    script.type = 'text/javascript';
    script.defer = true;
    document.getElementsByTagName('head').item(0).appendChild(script);
}

	var cpwmOpinion = "";
	cpwmOpinion = '<a href="#" onclick="OOo.launchFooterFeedback(event);"><div class="ml-icon ml-social-icon ml-icon-opinion-us ml-footer-c-icon visible-xs visible-sm visible-md visibleTab"><div>Feedback</div></div></a><style>.clearmyrow::after{clear:both;}footer .ml-icon.ml-icon-opinion-us {font-style:normal;font-weight:normal;}footer .ml-icon.ml-icon-opinion-us::before {content: " ";background: url(/images/integrations/opinionlab/oo_float_icon.png) no-repeat;width: 27px;height: 24px;display: block;}@media (min-width: 993px) and (max-width: 1024px) {.visibleTab{display:block !important;}}</style>';
	function incOLmobCpwm(){
		var olabDetect = setInterval(function () {
			var mainol = typeof OOo;
			if(mainol !== "undefined"){
				if(typeof OOo.__detectBrowser == 'function'){
					var Odetect = {};
					Odetect = OOo.__detectBrowser(navigator.userAgent);
//					console.log("HELLO! " + OOo.__detectBrowser(navigator.userAgent).isMobile);
					if(OOo.__detectBrowser(navigator.userAgent).isMobile){
//						console.log("MOBILE? " + OOo.__detectBrowser(navigator.userAgent).isMobile);
						if(jQuery("#ml-footer-contact-wrapper > a:nth-of-type(4)").length == 0){
							jQuery("#oo_tab.oo_tab_right").css('display','none');
							jQuery("#ml-footer-contact-wrapper > a:nth-of-type(3)").before("<div id='olMobile' class='visible-xs clearmyrow'></div>");
							jQuery("#ml-footer-contact-wrapper > a:nth-of-type(3)").after(cpwmOpinion);
						}
					} else if(!(OOo.__detectBrowser(navigator.userAgent).isMobile)) {
						jQuery("#oo_tab.oo_tab_right").css('display','block');
					}
					clearInterval(olabDetect);
				}
			}
		}, 1000);
	}

function cpwmLocalStore() {
	var cpwmLocalCheck = jQuery("#storeLink").html();
	console.log(cpwmLocalCheck + ": cpwmLocalCheck");
	var cpwmLimit = 0;

		if(cpwmLimit < 12){
			if(cpwmLocalCheck.length > 0) {
				cpwmLinkLocal = cpwmLocalCheck + "?ab=promo_carousel:11:1:local-store";
				jQuery(".cpwm-offer.cpwm-left a").attr("href",cpwmLinkLocal);
				jQuery("#promoslot-gps a.cpwm-store").attr("href",cpwmLinkLocal);
				clearInterval(cpwmLocalAvailable);
			}
		} else {
			clearInterval(cpwmLocalAvailable);
		}
	}, 1000);

              //holiday banner
function bannerdetails(){
	var bannerCTA = jQuery(".showbannerdisclaimer");
	var bannermodalDisclaimer = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.bannerdisclaimer");
	var bannercloseBtn = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.bannerdisclaimer");
	bannerCTA.click(function(){
//		console.log("BANNER CLICK");
		bannermodalDisclaimer.show();
	});
	bannercloseBtn.click(function(){
		bannermodalDisclaimer.hide();
	});
}

function cpwmDisclaimersAction(){
    var detailsCTA = jQuery(".promo-directory .promoslot .promodetails, .promo-header .promoslot .promodetails, .directorydisclaimer, .shareddisclaimer, .discountdetails, #see-details, #globalHeaderIncludeSm .shareddisclaimer");

	var alternatemodalDisclaimer = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.alternatedisclaimer");
    var additionaldetailsCTA = jQuery(".additionaldetails");
    var additionaldetailsTwoCTA = jQuery(".additionaldetails2");
    var frsdetailsCTA = jQuery(".frsdetails");
    var frspromodetailsCTA = jQuery(".frspromodetails");
    var curb10detailsCTA = jQuery(".curb10details");
	var additionalmodalDisclaimer = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.additionaldisclaimer");
	var additionalmodalDisclaimerTwo = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.additionaldisclaimer2");
	var frsmodalDisclaimer = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.frsdisclaimer");
	var frspromomodalDisclaimer = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.frspromodisclaimer");
	var curb10modalDisclaimer = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.curb10disclaimer");
    var sheeridCTA = jQuery(".sheeriddetails");
	var sheeridmodalDisclaimer = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.sheeriddisclaimer");
    var sheeridHealthcareCTA = jQuery(".cpwm-healthcare");
	var sheeridmodalHealthcare = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.sheeridhealthcare");
    var sheeridResponderCTA = jQuery(".cpwm-responder");
	var sheeridmodalResponder = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.sheeridresponder");
    var sheeridTeacherCTA = jQuery(".cpwm-teacher");
	var sheeridmodalTeacher = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.sheeridteacher");
    var pledgelingDonateCTA = jQuery(".cpwm-pledgeling-donate");
	var pledgelingmodalDonate = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.pledgelingdonate");
	
	var closeBtn = jQuery(".cpwm-promo-modal.disclaimer, .cpwm-promo-modal.alternatedisclaimer, .cpwm-promo-modal.additionaldisclaimer, .cpwm-promo-modal.additionaldisclaimer2, .cpwm-promo-modal.frsdisclaimer, .cpwm-promo-modal.frspromodisclaimer, .cpwm-promo-modal.curb10disclaimer, .cpwm-promo-modal.sheeriddisclaimer, .cpwm-promo-modal.sheeridhealthcare, .cpwm-promo-modal.sheeridresponder, .cpwm-promo-modal.sheeridteacher, .cpwm-promo-modal.pledgelingdonate");
    detailsCTA.click(function(){

        modalDisclaimer.show();
		jQuery(".disclaimer .close").focus();
		jQuery("#topmostHeader").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#ml-grid-view-subcatitems").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery(".breadcrumb").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#thSignIn").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#globalBasket").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
    });
    alternatedetailsCTA.click(function(){
//		console.log("Alternate Disclaimer Click");
        alternatemodalDisclaimer.show();
		jQuery(".alternatedisclaimer .close").focus();
		jQuery("#topmostHeader").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#ml-grid-view-subcatitems").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery(".breadcrumb").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#thSignIn").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#globalBasket").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
    });
    additionaldetailsCTA.click(function(){
//		console.log("Additional Details Click");
        additionalmodalDisclaimer.show();
		jQuery(".additionaldisclaimer .close").focus();
		jQuery("#topmostHeader").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#ml-grid-view-subcatitems").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery(".breadcrumb").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#thSignIn").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#globalBasket").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
    });
    additionaldetailsTwoCTA.click(function(){
//		console.log("Additional Details 2 Click");
        additionalmodalDisclaimerTwo.show();
		jQuery(".additionaldisclaimer2 .close").focus();
		jQuery("#topmostHeader").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#ml-grid-view-subcatitems").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery(".breadcrumb").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#thSignIn").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#globalBasket").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
    });
    frsdetailsCTA.click(function(){

        frsmodalDisclaimer.show();
		jQuery(".frsdisclaimer .close").focus();
		jQuery("#topmostHeader").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");
		jQuery("#ml-grid-view-subcatitems").addClass("cpwm-popup-compensate");

function getStateFromDomHeader() {
    var state = '';
    var address2 = jQuery(".eslAddress2").html();
    if(address2 != undefined && address2 != "undefined" && address2 != '') {
        var addressToken = address2.split(" ");
        if(addressToken != null && (addressToken.length > 2)) {
            state = addressToken[addressToken.length - 2]
        }
    }
    return state;
}

     <script>
      var glc = jQuery("#globalHeaderInclude").html();
	var h = jQuery("<div></div>").html(glc);
	jQuery(h).find("script").remove();
	jQuery(h).find("style").remove();
	jQuery(h).find("link").remove();
	jQuery('#globalHeaderIncludeSm').html(h.html());
	var deviceWidth = $(window).width();
	if(deviceWidth <= 992){
		$("#navsearchbox").focus(function(e){
	        $(".ml-header-search-btn-wrapper").addClass("focused");
	        $("#searchBtn").hide();
	        $("#clearBtn").show();
	        $(".search-overlay-bg").show();
	        $('body').addClass("search-modal");
	        $('html').addClass("search-html");
	    });
	    $("#navsearchbox").blur(function(e){
	    	setTimeout(function(){
	    		$(".ml-header-search-btn-wrapper").removeClass("focused");
		        $(".search-overlay-bg").hide();
		        $("#searchBtn").show();
		        $("#clearBtn").hide();
	    	},100);	        
	    });
	}
	$("#navsearchbox").focus(function(e){
		$("#navsearchbox").addClass("expended");
	});
	$("body").click(function(e){
		if(e.target.className != "ml-category-nav-arrow open"){
			$("#navsearchbox").removeClass("expended");
			$(".search-overlay-bg").hide();
			$("#searchBtn").show();
			$("#clearBtn").hide();
		}
	})
	$("#clearBtn").click(function(){
		$("#navsearchbox").val('');
	})
	$("#searchDiv").click(function(e){
		e.stopPropagation();
	})
	$(".ml-header-links-wrapper .ml-header-link-item").click(function(){
		$("#searchDiv .autocomplete.dropdown-menu").hide();
	})
     </script>
     <script>
      var windowWidth = $(window).width();
var headerdistance = 0;
sessionStorage.setItem("cartType", "new");
var fixmeTop;	
	if(windowWidth <= 640){
		fixmeTop = $('#globalHeaderIncludeSm').height();
	}else if(windowWidth > 641 && windowWidth <= 992){
		fixmeTop = $('#globalHeaderInclude').height();		
	}
    else{
		fixmeTop = 5;
		headerdistance = fixmeTop;
		/*if($('#storeClerkToolBar').length==0){
			$('#topmostHeader').css({'position':'fixed'});
		}*/
	}
	
	
function fixMe(){
		var currentScroll = window.pageYOffset;
		if(currentScroll >= fixmeTop){
			$("#ml-body-container").addClass("mobileFixMe");
			if(windowWidth <= 992){
			  //var sliderheight = window.screen.height - headerdistance ;
			 //$('#ml-nav-menu-left-slider').css({'height':sliderheight});	
			}
			else{
			   $('#ml-nav-menu-left-slider').css({'height':'auto'});
			}
		}
		else{
			$("#ml-body-container").removeClass("mobileFixMe");	
		}
}
$(window).scroll(function() {
	if(!$("#ml-nav-menu-left-slider.active").length)
		fixMe();
});
$(window).resize(function() {
	windowWidth = $(window).width();
	if(windowWidth <= 640){
		fixmeTop = $('#globalHeaderIncludeSm').height();
		headerdistance = 112;
		 var sliderheight = window.screen.height - headerdistance ;
		 $('#ml-nav-menu-left-slider').css({'height':sliderheight});	
	}
	else if(windowWidth > 641 && windowWidth <= 992){
		fixmeTop = 40;//$('#topmostHeader').height();
		headerdistance = 117;
		 var sliderheight = window.screen.height - headerdistance ;
		 $('#ml-nav-menu-left-slider').css({'height':sliderheight});	
	}
	else if(windowWidth > 992){
		fixmeTop = 5;
		headerdistance = fixmeTop;
		/*if($('#storeClerkToolBar').length==0){
			$('#topmostHeader').css({'position':'fixed'});
		}*/
	}
});

$(document).ready(function(){
	$(".ml-header-link-item.ml-menu-disabled").css("opacity",1);
	var flatShipChargeApplicable = ("false" == 'true');
	MarketLive.Base.setFlatShipChargeApplicable(flatShipChargeApplicable);	
	MarketLive.Base.refreshGlobalCart();
});

        <script>
         function closeUp(){
//Clicking 'Manage Preferences'; Closes 'notify' modal
		console.log("PREFERENCES LINK CLICKED");
		jQuery("#ensNotifyBanner").hide();
  	}
	function closePreferences() {
		jQuery("#ensCancel > div:nth-child(1)").click();
	}
	jQuery(document).keyup(function(e) {
		if (e.key === "Escape") { 
			console.log("CCPA Escape");
			jQuery("#ensCancel > div:nth-child(1)").click();
		}
	});	

	jQuery(document).ready(function(){
		var cpwmMNA = jQuery.cookie("COSTPLUSWORLDMARKET_ENSIGHTEN_PRIVACY_Marketing_and_Advertising");
		console.log("cpwmMNA: " + cpwmMNA);
		if(cpwmMNA == "0" || cpwmMNA == "1"){
			jQuery.cookie("COSTPLUSWORLDMARKET_ENSIGHTEN_PRIVACY_BANNER_VIEWED","1");
		}
		var isitthere = "#ensBannerDescription > p:nth-child(3) > a:nth-child(1)";
		var cpwmCloseEcks = '<span class="close" onclick="closePreferences();">&times;</span>';
		var isitthereChk = setInterval(function () {
			if(jQuery(isitthere).length > 0){
				jQuery("#ensBannerDescription > p:nth-child(3) > a:nth-child(1)").attr("onclick","closeUp()");
				jQuery("section#ensModalWrapper").prepend(cpwmCloseEcks);
//Clicking 'Cancel'; Closes 'preferences' modal
				jQuery("#ensCancel > div:nth-child(1)").click(function() {
					console.log("CANCEL CLICKED");
					jQuery("#ensModalWrapper").hide();
					if(!(jQuery.cookie("COSTPLUSWORLDMARKET_ENSIGHTEN_PRIVACY_Marketing_and_Advertising")) && (jQuery.cookie("COSTPLUSWORLDMARKET_ENSIGHTEN_PRIVACY_BANNER_VIEWED") != "1")){
						jQuery("#ensNotifyBanner").show();
					}
				});
//Clicking 'Save'; Closes 'preferences' modal
				jQuery("#ensSave > div:nth-child(1)").click(function() {
					console.log("SAVE CLICKED");
					jQuery("#ensModalWrapper").hide();
				});
				clearInterval(isitthereChk );
			}
		}, 1000);
	});
        </script>

              <script>
               // Function Include - General Utility to include a javascript file
// should be integrated with global.js when ready
function include(file) {
    var script  = document.createElement('script');
    script.src  = file;
    script.type = 'text/javascript';
    script.defer = true;
    document.getElementsByTagName('head').item(0).appendChild(script);
}

// Load pdp-popups.js if (1) we are on a Product Description Page AND (2) file has not already been loaded.
	jQuery(document).ready(function() {
	var found = jQuery('script[src*="pdp-popups.js"]').length != 0;

	var isProp65Type = pageData.page.type;
    if ((isProp65Type == "pdp" || isProp65Type == "product" || isProp65Type == "category" || isProp65Type == "gateway") && (!found)) {
        console.log("pdp-popups.js 2021.01.20 footer revise sms0120");
        include('/text/inc/js/pdp-popups.js?revise=sms0120');
    }
});

            jQuery(".logged").hide();

            jQuery(".cpwm-kiosk").show();
        }
    });

      <script defer="true" type="text/javascript">
       $(document).ready(function() {
  //toggle the component with class accordion_body
	$(".ml-accordion-footer").click(function() {
	    if ($(this).parents(".ml-footer-links-section").children("ul").children(".footerItem").is(':visible')) {
	        $(this).parents(".ml-footer-links-section").children("ul").children(".footerItem").slideUp(300);
	        $(this).removeClass("ml-accordion-footer-active");
	    }else{
	        $(this).parents(".ml-footer-links-section").children("ul").children(".footerItem").slideDown(300);
	        $(this).addClass("ml-accordion-footer-active");
	    }
	  });
});
      </script>

           function isLogged() {

        if(loggedStatus == "registered") {
            jQuery(".nonwme").hide();
            jQuery(".wme").hide();

        isLogged();

   <script>
    var LiveChatManager = {
	//CompatibleURL:["/category/customer-service","/home"],
	CompatibleURL:["/category/customer-service", "/category/code/in-store-pick-up.do"],
	show:function(){
		if(LiveChatManager.isCompatiblePage()){
			jQuery("#livechat-links-cpwm").show();
			jQuery("#livechat-links-cpwm a").click(function(event){
				event.preventDefault();
				//LiveChatManager.open();
			});
		}
	},
	isCompatiblePage:function(){
		var compatible = false;
		if(MarketLive.Base.isAOSMode || MarketLive.Base.isKioskMode)
			return compatible;
		if(window.location.pathname=='/' || window.location.pathname.indexOf('/home') != -1){
			return true;
		}
		if(LiveChatManager.CompatibleURL){
			for(i=0;i<LiveChatManager.CompatibleURL.length;i++){
				if(window.location.pathname.indexOf(LiveChatManager.CompatibleURL[i]) != -1){
					compatible=true;
					break;
				}
			}
		}
		return compatible;
	}
	/* open:function(){
		window.open('/livechat.do','LiveChatCPWM','scrollbars=no,resizable=no,status=no,location=no,toolbar=no,menubar=no,width=400,height=690')
	} */
}
LiveChatManager.show();
   </script>

if(type=='coupons' || type=='content' || tmpCurCatid.length < 1 || tmpCurl.indexOf('/emailSignup/thankyou') !=-1 || tmpCurCatid.indexOf('worldmarket') !=-1 || type=='customer service') {
	if(type=='content' && MarketLive.Reporting.dlGlobal.dirItemsArray.length > 1){
		prodArrayHolder=MarketLive.Reporting.dlGlobal.dirItemsArray;
	}else{
		if(type.indexOf('shopping') !=-1){
		}else{
			delete pageArr['categoryId'];
		}
	}
}
if(type=='shopping cart') {
	delete pageArr['subtype'];
}
if(pgName.length < 1) 
		delete pageArr['name'];
	
if(ensSearchRedirectTerm.length < 1) 
		delete pageArr['searchRedirectTerm'];	
	
if(pageCouponArr.length < 1) 
		delete pageArr['couponCodes'];
//clean up as per new version doc	
if(type=='home_page' || type=='gateway' || type=='search' || type=='search results'){
	delete pageArr['searchRedirectTerm'];
	if(type=='home_page' || type=='gateway'){
		delete pageArr['subtype'];
		if(type=='gateway'){
			delete pageArr['subCategories'];
		}
	}
}
if(tmpCurl.indexOf('/content/') !=-1){
	if(type.indexOf('shopping') !=-1){
	}else{
		delete pageArr['categoryId'];
		delete pageArr['productCategories'];
	}
}
if(tmpCurl.indexOf('/inspirations/') !=-1 || tmpCurl.indexOf('/email-signup') !=-1){
	delete pageArr['categoryId'];
}	

if(type=='category'){
	delete pageArr['subtype'];
}
if(pcats.length < 1 || type=='shopping cart' || type=='pdp' || type=='search' || type=='search results') {
	if(subtype !=='pla')
		delete pageArr['productCategories'];
}
if(psubcats.length < 1 || type=='shopping cart' || type=='pdp') {
	delete pageArr['subCategories'];
}

if(type=='pdp') {
	prodArrayHolder=MarketLive.Reporting.dlGlobal.ensPDPSkusArray;
	if(subtype=='pla' && prodDirList.length > 1){
		var placoncat=prodArrayHolder.concat(prodDirList);
		prodArrayHolder=placoncat;
	}

}
if(tmpCurl.indexOf('/search') !=-1){
	
}
var ensItemCnt ={
	"totalResults":ensProdCnt,
	"facets":pageFacetsArr,
	"currentPage":ensPageCnt
}
 if(pageFacetsArr.length < 1)
 {
	ensItemCnt =
	{
	"totalResults":ensProdCnt,
	"currentPage":ensPageCnt
	}
} 
 
var pageData =
{
	"customer":customerArr,
	"form":formErrObj,
	"order":pageOrderObj,
    "page":pageArr,
	"productList":ensItemCnt,
	"products":prodArrayHolder
}

if(type=='coupons' || type=='error' || prodArrayHolder.length < 1) {
	delete pageData['products'];
}

if(type !='shopping cart' && (type !='checkout' && type!='order confirmation')) {
	delete pageData['order'];
}
 
if(ensProdCnt < 1) {
	delete pageData['productList'];
}
if(formErrObj.length < 1) {
	delete pageData['form'];
}
 
console.log(JSON.stringify(pageData));
console.log('**** DataLayer - Ensighten Reporting - End ****');

    jQuery(window).add(document).on('ready resize load', function() {
         var bufInMod = 45;
        if(MarketLive.Base.isExtraSmall()) {
            var sL = jQuery("#thSignIn").offset().left;
            var wW = jQuery(window).width();
            var ww = jQuery("#thSignIn .dropdown-wrapper").width();
            var xP = (( wW - ww )/2) - sL;
            jQuery("#thSignIn .dropdown-wrapper").css("left",xP+"px");
			if(!jQuery("#thSignIn .dropdown-wrapper").is(":visible")){
				jQuery(".loggedIn").removeClass("openMenu");
				jQuery('body').removeClass("open-Amenu");	
			}
            bufInMod = 0;
        }
        else{
            jQuery("#thSignIn .dropdown-wrapper").removeAttr("style");
            bufInMod = 45;
        }

    });

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
			var currentParentCategoryCode = '';
			var currentChildCategoryCode = '';
			var currentParentCategoryName = '',
				currentChildCategoryName = '',
				topStaticNav = $('#desktpNav .ml-navbar-menu');

			function activeFlatStaticMenus() {
				topStaticNav.each(function () {
					var menuElement = $(this), $activeRootCat = $activeSubCat = '';
					if(currentParentCategoryName != undefined && currentParentCategoryName != ''){
						menuElement.find('.ml-sibling-group-root').each(function () {
							$activeRootCat = $(this).find('a:first').text();
							if($activeRootCat.match("^" + currentParentCategoryName + "$") !== null){
								$(this).addClass('active');
							}

							if($(this).hasClass('active') && currentChildCategoryName != undefined && currentChildCategoryName != ''){
								var $subMenu = $(this).find('ul li.ml-sibling-group li');
								$subMenu.each(function(){
									$activeSubCat = $(this).find('a:first').text();
									if($activeSubCat.match("^" + currentChildCategoryName + "$") !== null){
										$(this).addClass('active');
									}
								});
							}
						});
					}					
				});
			}
			$( window ).load(function() {
				activeFlatStaticMenus();          
			});
		});
   </script>

			var isLoggedInUser = 'false';
			var isMergedUser = '';
			var isKoiskMode = 'false';
			var isAOSMode = 'false';
			var wmeNumber = '';
			var isAosRecaptchaEnabled = '';
			
			MarketLive.Base.initLoginStatus(isLoggedInUser, isMergedUser, isKoiskMode, isAOSMode, wmeNumber,isAosRecaptchaEnabled);
	});
	
	 var loginCheck = function(){
	 
  		var locationHref = window.location.href;
		var isLoggedInUser = 'false';
		var forwardPage = '';
			
		if(isLoggedInUser == 'false') {
			//MarketLive.Base.resetLoginRecaptcha();
			if(locationHref.indexOf("pagetype=createaccount") != -1) {
				MarketLive.Base.showCreateAccount(forwardPage);
			}else if(locationHref.indexOf("pagetype=completeaccount") != -1 || locationHref.indexOf("signin=store") != -1) {
				MarketLive.Base.showCompleteProfile(forwardPage);
			}else if(locationHref.indexOf("pagetype=signin") != -1 || locationHref.indexOf("signin=on") != -1) {
				MarketLive.Base.openSignInPopUp(forwardPage);
			}else if(locationHref.indexOf("pagetype=accountsupport") != -1) {
				MarketLive.Base.showCustomerSupport();
				MarketLive.Reporting.dlGlobal.overlayFormOpen('account support');
			} else if(locationHref.indexOf("pagetype=passwordreset") != -1) {
				MarketLive.Base.showPasswordReset();
				MarketLive.Reporting.dlGlobal.overlayFormOpen('password reset');
			}			
		} else {
			if(locationHref.indexOf("pagetype=accountsupport") != -1) {
				MarketLive.Base.showCustomerSupport();
				MarketLive.Reporting.dlGlobal.overlayFormOpen('account support');
			}
			else if(locationHref.indexOf("pagetype=kiboonly") != -1) {
				MarketLive.Base.showJoinNowModal(forwardPage);
			}
		}
	}

	 function invokePopup(url) {

	 }

		event.stopPropagation();
		if($(this).find(".pop-over").eq(0).is(":visible")){
			$(this).find(".pop-over").eq(0).hide();
		} else {
			$('.pop-over').hide();
			$(this).find(".pop-over").eq(0).show();
		}
	});

   		// remove any active menu	
   		jQuery('.ml-megamenu').find("li.ml-category-nav-item.active").removeClass("active");		
   		var menuItem = 'li.ml-category-nav-item.ml-category-nav-id-' + currentCatCode;
   		jQuery('.ml-megamenu').find(menuItem).addClass("active");
   		jQuery('.ml-megamenu').find(menuItem).closest("li.ml-sibling-group-root" ).addClass("active");
   	}
   	
	    $( document ).ready(function() {
				if(!$("body").hasClass('ml-wishlist-enabled')) {
					$("body").addClass('ml-wishlist-enabled');
				}
	    	});
	
	if($('.ml-navleft-subCats-active').length>=1){
		$('.ml-navleft-subCats-active ul a').attr('aria-current','page');
	}else if($('.ml-navleft-cats-active').length>=1){
		$('.ml-navleft-cats-active ul a').not('.glyphicon').attr('aria-current','page');
	}
   </script>
  </div>
 </body>
</html>
